<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">восхвали́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vosxvalítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***восхитить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:восхитить.html>восхи́тить</a> (26026)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">въсхытити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vŭsxytiti</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to fascinate, to snatch away</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:восхитить.html>восхити́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vosxitítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:восхищать.html>восхища́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to enrapture, to delight, to ravish</li></ol>

<p><b>вос<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>хи<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ща́ть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. ***восходить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:восходить.html>восходи́ть</a> (16305)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:восходить.html>восходи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vosxodítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взойти.html>взойти́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to ascend, to climb, to go up, to mount</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">imperfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to go back (to a particular time)</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>вос<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>хо<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ди́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4c.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:взойти.html>взойти́</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> знач. 1 <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> 2).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>вос-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-ход-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:восьмерка.html>восьмёрка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vosʹmjórka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:восьмерка.html>восьмёрки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:восьмерка.html>восьмёрки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:восьмерка.html>восьмёрок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>number eight, eight (e.g. cards), figure of eight</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">card games</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> eight
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:козырной.html>козырна́я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:восьмерка.html>восьмёрка</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kozyrnája <b>vosʹmjórka</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the eight of trumps</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>No 8 bus, tram, etc</li></ol>

***восьмеро.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:восьмеро.html>во́сьмеро</a> (30755)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:восьмеро.html>во́сьмеро</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vósʹmero</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>eight (in a group together), eight of them
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:восьмеро.html>во́сьмеро</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>дете́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vósʹmero</b> detéj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">eight children</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:восьмеро.html>во́сьмеро</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часо́в</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vósʹmero</b> časóv</i> ― <span class="e-translation">eight watches</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:восьмеро.html>во́сьмеро</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>очко́в</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vósʹmero</b> očkóv</i> ― <span class="e-translation">eight pairs of glasses</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:восьмеро.html>во́сьмеро</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нас</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vósʹmero</b> iz nas</i> ― <span class="e-translation">eight of us</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нас</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:восьмеро.html>во́сьмеро</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nas býlo <b>vósʹmero</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">there were eight of us</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The nominative of a collective numeral governs the genitive plural of the noun, pronoun, or adjective. The other cases agree with that of the noun, pronoun, or adjective. Not used with feminine nouns. Used mostly when speaking of children and with a few nouns that are used in the plural only, such as <a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часы́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>очки́</a>, or with pronouns.
</p>

<p><b>во́сь<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ме<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ро</b>
</p><p>Числительное, <a href = vnd.unilang:собирательный.html>собира́тельное</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-восьм-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ер</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-о</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>вось<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>мо́й</a></b>
</p><p>Числительное, <a href = vnd.unilang:порядковый.html>поря́дковое</a>, адъективное <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1b. <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующее</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:количественный.html>коли́чественное</a> числительное — <a href = vnd.unilang:восемь.html>восемь</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-восьм-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ой</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

***вот.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вот.html>вот</a> (47)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:ото.html>ото</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oto</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">вото</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">voto</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, compare with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">oto</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Particle">Particle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вот.html>вот</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vot</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>here (is), this (is)
<dl><dd><ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вот.html>Вот</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>мой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>дом</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Vot</b> moj dom.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Here/this is my house.</span></div></li></ul></dd></dl></li>
<li>there
<dl><dd><ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вот.html>Вот</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>тебе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>раз</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Vot</b> tebé raz!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">There you are!</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вот.html>Вот</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Vot</b> i vsjó!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">That’s all!</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вот.html>Вот</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Vot</b> čelovék!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">What a man!</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вот.html>во́т</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:где.html>где</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vót</b> gde</i> ― <span class="e-translation">here’s where</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">вот-во́т</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vot-vót</i> ― <span class="e-translation">just about to; on the point of</span></div></li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вот.html>вот</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vot</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>here, look (at it)</li>
<li>take it! (when offering something, casual)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:наречие.html>Наре́чие</a>, местоименное, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вводный.html>вво́дная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:частица.html>части́ца</a>; неизменяемое.

</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вошедший.html>воше́дший</a> (398)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вошедший.html>воше́дший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vošédšij</span>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вошь.html>вошь</a> (19051)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*vъšь</i>.
</p>

</p>

***впадать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:впадать.html>впада́ть</a> (6953)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">впад-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vpad-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:впадать.html>впада́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vpadátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:впасть.html>впа́сть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>(river)</i> to fall <i>(into)</i>, to flow <i>(into)</i></li>
<li><i>(a condition)</i> to fall <i>(into)</i>, to lapse <i>(into)</i>, to sink <i>(into)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:впадать.html>впада́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:задумчивость.html>заду́мчивость</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vpadátʹ</b> v zadúmčivostʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fall into a reverie</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:впадать.html>впада́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отчаяние.html>отча́яние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vpadátʹ</b> v otčájanije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give way to despair; be driven into despair</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:впадать.html>впада́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сомнение.html>сомне́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vpadátʹ</b> v somnénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to begin to have doubts</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:впадать.html>впада́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> неми́лость</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vpadátʹ</b> v nemílostʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fall into disfavour/disgrace</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:впадать.html>впада́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:детство.html>де́тство</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vpadátʹ</b> v détstvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to enter one's second childhood; be in one's dotage</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:впадать.html>впада́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:противоречие.html>противоре́чие</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vpadátʹ</b> v protivoréčije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">contradict oneself</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(cheeks, eyes etc.)</i> to sink in, to become hollow/sunken</li></ol>

<p><b>впа<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>да́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:впасть.html>впасть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:невдомек.html>в-</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-пад-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***впасть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:впасть.html>впасть</a> (7546)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невдомек.html>в-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пасть.html>пасть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pastʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:впасть.html>впасть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vpastʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:впадать.html>впада́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>(river)</i> to fall <i>(into)</i>, to flow <i>(into)</i></li>
<li><i>(a condition)</i> to fall <i>(into)</i>, to lapse <i>(into)</i>, to sink <i>(into)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:впасть.html>впасть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:задумчивость.html>заду́мчивость</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vpastʹ</b> v zadúmčivostʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fall into a reverie</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:впасть.html>впасть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отчаяние.html>отча́яние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vpastʹ</b> v otčájanije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give way to despair; be driven into despair</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:впасть.html>впасть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сомнение.html>сомне́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vpastʹ</b> v somnénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to begin to have doubts</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:впасть.html>впасть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> неми́лость</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vpastʹ</b> v nemílostʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fall into disfavour/disgrace</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:впасть.html>впасть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:детство.html>де́тство</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vpastʹ</b> v détstvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to enter one's second childhood; be in one's dotage</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:впасть.html>впасть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:противоречие.html>противоре́чие</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vpastʹ</b> v protivoréčije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">contradict oneself</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(cheeks, eyes etc.)</i> to sink in, to become hollow/sunken</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:впалый.html>впа́лый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vpályj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
